<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/tre#Middle_English" title="tre">tre</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/tree#Middle_English" title="tree">tree</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/treo#Middle_English" title="treo">treo</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/treou#Middle_English" title="treou">treou</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/trew#Middle_English" title="trew">trew</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/trow#Middle_English" title="trow">trow</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/treo#Old_English" title="treo">trēo</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/treow#Old_English" title="treow">trēow</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree, wood, timber, beam, log, stake, stick, grove, cross, rood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/treu" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/treu">*treu</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/trew%C4%85" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/trewą">*trewą</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree, wood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from pre-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dr%C3%A9wom&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dréwom (page does not exist)">*dréwom</a></i>, thematic e-grade derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/d%C3%B3ru" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/dóru">*dóru</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/tɹiː/</span>, <span class="IPA">[t̠ɹ̠̊˔ʷɪi̯]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_American" class="extiw" title="w:General American">General American</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">trē</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/tɹi/</span>, <span class="IPA">[t̠ɹ̠̊˔ʷi]</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">tree</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/trees#English" title="trees">trees</a></b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/treen#English" title="treen">treen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href="/wiki/perennial" title="perennial">perennial</a> <a href="/wiki/woody" title="woody">woody</a> <a href="/wiki/plant" title="plant">plant</a>, not exactly defined, but differentiated from a <a href="/wiki/shrub" title="shrub">shrub</a> by its larger size (typically over a few meters in height) or growth habit, usually having a single (or few) main <a href="/wiki/axis" title="axis">axis</a> or <a href="/wiki/trunk" title="trunk">trunk</a> unbranched for some distance above the ground and a head of branches and foliage.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Hyperion is the tallest living <b>tree</b> in the world.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Birds have a nest in a <b>tree</b> in the garden.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1992</b> April 5, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Jeeves_and_Wooster_episodes" class="extiw" title="w:List of Jeeves and Wooster episodes">"The Full House"</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jeeves_and_Wooster" class="extiw" title="w:Jeeves and Wooster"><i>Jeeves and Wooster</i></a>, Series 3, Episode 2:
<dl><dd><i>B. Wooster:</i> Of all the places on this great planet of ours, West Neck, Long Island, has chosen to be the most unexciting. The last time anything <i>remotely</i> interesting happened here was in 1842, when a <b>tree</b> fell over. They still talk about it in the village.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2019</b> October,  Ian Walmsley,  “Cleaning up”, in  <cite>Modern Railways</cite>, page 42:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">When we see a train trapped behind (or embedded in) a fallen <b>tree</b> our first thought should be 'what was it doing there anyway?' <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span><b>Trees</b> are also responsible for numerous minor delays in autumn <small>[due to leaves falling on the track]</small>, which rolling stock engineers are supposed to cope with as usual.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any <a href="/wiki/plant" title="plant">plant</a> that is <a href="/wiki/reminiscent" title="reminiscent">reminiscent</a> of the above but not <a href="/wiki/classified" title="classified">classified</a> as a tree (in any <a href="/wiki/botanical" title="botanical">botanical</a> sense).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">the banana <b>tree</b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>An object made from a tree trunk and having multiple <a href="/wiki/hook" title="hook">hooks</a> or storage <a href="/wiki/platform" title="platform">platforms</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He had the choice of buying a scratching post or a cat <b>tree</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A device used to hold or stretch a shoe open.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He put a shoe <b>tree</b> in each of his shoes.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The structural <a href="/wiki/frame" title="frame">frame</a> of a <a href="/wiki/saddle" title="saddle">saddle</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/graph_theory" title="graph theory">graph theory</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A connected <a href="/wiki/graph" title="graph">graph</a> with no cycles or, if the graph is finite, equivalently a connected graph with <i>n</i> vertices and <i>n</i>−1 edges.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/computing#Noun" title="computing">computing</a> <a href="/wiki/theory" title="theory">theory</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/recursive" title="recursive">recursive</a> <a href="/wiki/data_structure" title="data structure">data structure</a> in which each <a href="/wiki/node" title="node">node</a> has zero or more nodes as children.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/graphical_user_interface" title="graphical user interface">graphical user interface</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/display" title="display">display</a> or listing of <a href="/wiki/entry" title="entry">entries</a> or <a href="/wiki/element" title="element">elements</a> such that there are <a href="/wiki/primary" title="primary">primary</a> and <a href="/wiki/secondary" title="secondary">secondary</a> entries shown, usually linked by drawn lines or by indenting to the right.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">We’ll show it as a <b>tree</b> list.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any <a href="/wiki/structure" title="structure">structure</a> or <a href="/wiki/construct" title="construct">construct</a> having <a href="/wiki/branch" title="branch">branches</a> representing <a href="/wiki/divergence" title="divergence">divergence</a> or possible <a href="/wiki/choice" title="choice">choices</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/family_tree#English" title="family tree">family tree</a>; <a href="/wiki/skill_tree#English" title="skill tree">skill tree</a></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English:_saddle"> The <a href="/wiki/structure" title="structure">structure</a> or <a href="/wiki/wooden" title="wooden">wooden</a> <a href="/wiki/frame" title="frame">frame</a> used in the construction of a <a href="/wiki/saddle" title="saddle">saddle</a> used in horse riding.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/marijuana" title="marijuana">Marijuana</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eminem" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Eminem">Eminem</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nate_Dogg" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nate Dogg">Nate Dogg</a> (lyrics),  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shake_That" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shake That">Shake That</a>”, in  <cite>Curtain Call: The Hits</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I like good pussy and I like good <b>trees</b> / Smoke so much weed you wouldn't believe</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b>,  “Ace Feat. Smino &amp; Saba”, in  <cite>Room 25</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://nonameraps.bandcamp.com/album/room-25">[1]</a></sup>, performed by Noname:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Whiskey with the team, got it bubblin' / I got <b>trees</b> in my luggage, I got tings out in London / Hope UK, what you say? Fuck is you sayin'?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/cross" title="cross">cross</a> or <a href="/wiki/gallows" title="gallows">gallows</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Tyburn <b>tree</b></i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1611</b>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bible" class="extiw" title="w:Bible">The Holy Bible,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&nbsp;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="Conteyning the Old Testament, and the New. <li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1610–1611</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="w:The Tempest">The Tempest</a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp; <li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/chemistry" title="chemistry">chemistry</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mass of <a href="/wiki/crystal" title="crystal">crystals</a>, <a href="/wiki/aggregate" title="aggregate">aggregated</a> in <a href="/wiki/arborescent" title="arborescent">arborescent</a> forms, obtained by <a href="/wiki/precipitation" title="precipitation">precipitation</a> of a <a href="/wiki/metal" title="metal">metal</a> from <a href="/wiki/solution" title="solution">solution</a>.</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in graph theory</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/graph#English" title="graph">graph</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hyponyms">Hyponyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Hyponyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="term-list-header">Of the sense “a perennial plant”</div><div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: #F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cabbage_tree#English" title="cabbage tree">cabbage tree</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/chaste_tree#English" title="chaste tree">chaste tree</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cherry_tree#English" title="cherry tree">cherry tree</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Cherry_Tree#English" title="Cherry Tree">Cherry Tree</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">places</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hip_tree#English" title="hip tree">hip tree</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Joshua_tree#English" title="Joshua tree">Joshua tree</a></span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: References">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tree_(disambiguation)" title="w:Tree (disambiguation)"><img alt="Wikipedia-logo.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/15px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="15" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/23px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/30px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></a> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tree_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:Tree (disambiguation)">Tree (disambiguation)</a></b> on  Wikipedia.<span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tree_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:Tree (disambiguation)">Wikipedia </a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">tree</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/trees#English" title="trees">trees</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/treeing#English" title="treeing">treeing</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/treed#English" title="treed">treed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To chase (an animal or person) up a tree.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The dog <b>treed</b> the cat.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1897</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Howard,_18th_Earl_of_Suffolk" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Howard, 18th Earl of Suffolk">Henry Howard</a> <i>et al.</i> (eds.), <i>Encyclopaedia of Sport</i>, London: Lawrence &amp; Bullen, Volume I, p. 599,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/encyclopaediaofs01suff">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>When hunted it [the jaguar] takes refuge in trees, and this habit is well known to hunters, who pursue it with dogs and pot it when <b>treed</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To place in a tree.
<dl><dd><i>Black bears can <b>tree</b> their cubs for protection, but grizzly bears cannot.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To place upon a tree; to fit with a tree; to stretch upon a tree.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">to <b>tree</b> a boot</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1930</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dashiell_Hammett" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Dashiell Hammett">Dashiell Hammett</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Maltese_Falcon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Maltese Falcon">The Maltese Falcon</a></i>, New York: Alfred A. Knopf, Chapter 14, p. 165,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/maltesefalcon01hamm">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Two suits and an overcoat hung in the closet over three pairs of carefully <b>treed</b> shoes.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To take refuge in a tree.</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Afrikaans">Afrikaans</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Afrikaans">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/tree#Dutch" title="tree">tree</a></i>, syncopic form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/trede#Dutch" title="trede">trede</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href="/wiki/trede#Middle_Dutch" title="trede">trede</a></i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/treden#Dutch" title="treden">treden</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="af">tree</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-af p-form-of" lang="af"><a href="/wiki/tre%C3%AB#Afrikaans" title="treë">treë</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/step#English" title="step">step</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">single act of placing the foot when walking</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/trede#Dutch" title="trede">trede</a></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From syncope of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/trede#Dutch" title="trede">trede</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href="/wiki/trede#Middle_Dutch" title="trede">trede</a></i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/treden#Dutch" title="treden">treden</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl">tree</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/treden#Dutch" title="treden">treden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/tree%C3%ABn#Dutch" title="treeën">treeën</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/trees#Dutch" title="trees">trees</a></b>, <i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#diminutive" title="Appendix:Glossary">diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/treetje#Dutch" title="treetje">treetje</a></b>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/step" title="step">step</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a <a href="/wiki/staircase" title="staircase">staircase</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <a href="/wiki/stair" title="stair">stair</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/step" title="step">step</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">distance of one step when walking</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/tred#Dutch" title="tred">tred</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a unit of length of about 2 to 3 <a href="/wiki/feet" title="feet">feet</a>, roughly equivalent to a <a href="/wiki/yard" title="yard">yard</a></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=tree&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga"><a href="/wiki/tr%C3%AD#Old_Irish" title="trí">trí</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/tr%C4%ABs" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/trīs">*trīs</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/tr%C3%A9yes" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/tréyes">*tréyes</a></i>.
</p>
